<span id="freeTextContainer3373087919361748641">I have a friend who contends that this is the greatest sci-fi book for young adults ever published. While I certainly agree that this is a fine book for that (and all) ages, particularly as it may be a useful teaching tool for certain history, social studies, and civics classes, I still think "Ender's Game" takes the cake.<br/><br/>The characters are well thought out and the plot is solid. I think there could be more galaxy gallivanting, maybe a few more episodes for young Thorby, but at the same time the</span>
  <span id="freeText3373087919361748641" style="display:none">I have a friend who contends that this is the greatest sci-fi book for young adults ever published. While I certainly agree that this is a fine book for that (and all) ages, particularly as it may be a useful teaching tool for certain history, social studies, and civics classes, I still think "Ender's Game" takes the cake.<br /><br />The characters are well thought out and the plot is solid. I think there could be more galaxy gallivanting, maybe a few more episodes for young Thorby, but at the same time the plot is fairly tight, and that feeling may just be the yearning I get with every book that I enjoy: I wish there was more. Of course Robert Heinlein did write another 45 or so books, and the other two of his that I've read "Starship Troopers" and "Tunnel in the Sky" I've also enjoyed. Orson Scott Card has written many novels as well, but I was never able to get into "Speaker For the Dead," and I feel as though my politics and particular sociological interests align somewhat more closely with those that seep into Heinlein novels. <br /><br />Certainly I feel I should read some more Heinlein. Any suggestions?</span>
  <a data-text-id="3373087919361748641" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_698472256" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/698472256" />
    <a title="Kat  Hooper" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2177891-kat-hooper"><img alt="Kat  Hooper" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533675060p2/2177891.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/698472256?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat  Hooper" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat  Hooper" href="/user/show/2177891-kat-hooper">Kat  Hooper</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2177891-kat-hooper?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer698472256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12230101741050569130">4.5 stars<br/><br/>Robert A. Heinlein’s best books are those he wrote for kids, and Citizen of the Galaxy is one of the best of those. Originally serialized in Astounding Science Fiction in 1957, this is an anthropological adventure story with strong libertarian and anti-slavery themes.<br/><br/>We first meet Thorby, a young belligerent orphaned slave boy, as he has just landed on an unfamiliar planet and is on the auction block. Nobody wants him — he’s too feisty — but he is eventually sold for a pittance to Basli</span>
  <span id="freeText12230101741050569130" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />Robert A. Heinlein’s best books are those he wrote for kids, and Citizen of the Galaxy is one of the best of those. Originally serialized in Astounding Science Fiction in 1957, this is an anthropological adventure story with strong libertarian and anti-slavery themes.<br /><br />We first meet Thorby, a young belligerent orphaned slave boy, as he has just landed on an unfamiliar planet and is on the auction block. Nobody wants him — he’s too feisty — but he is eventually sold for a pittance to Baslim, a man who appears to be a crippled beggar. Despite Baslim’s kind treatment, it takes a while for Thorby to warm up, but once he does he discovers that Baslim is more than he seems. Under Baslim’s tutorage, Thorby becomes an accomplished and very well educated beggar.<br /><br />Eventually Thorby must leave his new home, but the knowledge and connections he received from Baslim ... Read More at Fantasy Literature: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.fantasyliterature.com/reviews/citizen-of-the-galaxy/">http://www.fantasyliterature.com/revi...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12230101741050569130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Hhm5xZD2hCxCDuEOgf9q3MmTSNsmf7VKgfx1lWauWBOF2Wa1Lt8+dCtNCoQboCDhR+nw7Cp5wb7PNcjxKm/lfg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('atyl1wUCwxKLF97p160ba99GRPNpQG5iwv3doBsNLH7xHHqnuyt5SuJUNWNN8lFWUTz8xGVGGpaMNGDEV8yREw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer157634490625001783">Robert Anson Heinlein was an American novelist and science fiction writer. Often called "the dean of science fiction writers", he is one of the most popular, influential, and controversial authors of "hard science fiction". <br/><br/>He set a high standard for science and engineering plausibility and helped to raise the genre's standards of literary quality. He was the first SF writer to break into mainstre</span>
  <span id="freeText157634490625001783" style="display:none">Robert Anson Heinlein was an American novelist and science fiction writer. Often called "the dean of science fiction writers", he is one of the most popular, influential, and controversial authors of "hard science fiction". <br /><br />He set a high standard for science and engineering plausibility and helped to raise the genre's standards of literary quality. He was the first SF writer to break into mainstream, general magazines such as <i>The Saturday Evening Post</i>, in the late 1940s. He was also among the first authors of bestselling, novel-length science fiction in the modern, mass-market era. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="157634490625001783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
